   }\n\n    @Override\n    public Iterator<Record> iterator() {\n        if (count() == 0)\n            return Collections.emptyIterator();\n\n        if (!isCompressed())\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n\n        // for a normal iterator, we cannot ensure that the underlying compression stream is closed,\n        // so we decompress the full record set here. Use cases which call for a lower memory footprint\n        // can use `streamingIterator` at the cost of additional complexity\n        try (CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = compressedIterator(BufferSupplier.NO_CACHING, false)) {\n            List<Record> records = new ArrayList<>(count());\n            while (iterator.hasNext())\n                records.add(iterator.next());\n            return records.iterator();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a closeable iterator that skips over key/value/header data for efficiency.\n     *\n     * <p>This is used internally by log validators and other tools that need to access batch\n     * metadata without deserializing record contents. For compressed batches, this still requires\n     * decompression but avoids allocating buffers for key/value data.\n     *\n     * @param bufferSupplier The supplier of ByteBuffer(s) for decompression if needed\n     * @return A {@link CloseableIterator} over partially-read records. Must be closed.\n     */\n    public CloseableIterator<Record> skipKeyValueIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        if (count() == 0) {\n            return CloseableIterator.wrap(Collections.emptyIterator());\n        }\n\n        /*\n         * For uncompressed iterator, it is actually not worth skipping key / value / headers at all since\n         * its ByteBufferInputStream's skip() function is less efficient compared with just reading it actually\n         * as it will allocate new byte array.\n         */\n        if (!isCompressed())\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n\n        // we define this to be a closable iterator so that caller (i.e. the log validator) needs to close it\n        // while we can save memory footprint of not decompressing the full record set ahead of time\n        return compressedIterator(bufferSupplier, true);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public CloseableIterator<Record> streamingIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        if (isCompressed())\n            return compressedIterator(bufferSupplier, false);\n        else\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void setLastOffset(long offset) {\n        buffer.putLong(BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET, offset - lastOffsetDelta());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void setMaxTimestamp(TimestampType timestampType, long maxTimestamp) {\n        long currentMaxTimestamp = maxTimestamp();\n        // We don't need to recompute crc if the timestamp is not updated.\n        if (timestampType() == timestampType && currentMaxTimestamp == maxTimestamp)\n            return;\n\n        byte attributes = computeAttributes(compressionType(), timestampType, isTransactional(), isControlBatch(), hasDeleteHorizonMs());\n        buffer.putShort(ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, attributes);\n        buffer.putLong(MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET, maxTimestamp);\n        long crc = computeChecksum();\n        ByteUtils.writeUnsignedInt(buffer, CRC_OFFSET, crc);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void setPartitionLeaderEpoch(int epoch) {\n        buffer.putInt(PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET, epoch);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long checksum() {\n        return ByteUtils.readUnsignedInt(buffer, CRC_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    public boolean isValid() {\n        return sizeInBytes() >= RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD && checksum() == computeChecksum();\n    }\n\n    private long computeChecksum() {\n        return Crc32C.compute(buffer, ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, buffer.limit() - ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private byte attributes() {\n        // note we're not using the second byte of attributes\n        return (byte) buffer.getShort(ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean equals(Object o) {\n        if (this == o)\n            return true;\n        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass())\n            return false;\n\n        DefaultRecordBatch that = (DefaultRecordBatch) o;\n        return Objects.equals(buffer, that.buffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int hashCode() {\n        return buffer != null ? buffer.hashCode() : 0;\n    }\n\n    private static byte computeAttributes(CompressionType type, TimestampType timestampType,\n                                          boolean isTransactional, boolean isControl, boolean isDeleteHorizonSet) {\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Timestamp type must be provided to compute attributes for message \" +\n                    \"format v2 and above\");\n\n        byte attributes = isTransactional ? empty\n     */\n    public static int sizeInBytes(long baseOffset, Iterable<Record> records) {\n        Iterator<Record> iterator = records.iterator();\n        if (!iterator.hasNext())\n            return 0;\n\n        int size = RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD;\n        Long baseTimestamp = null;\n        while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n            Record record = iterator.next();\n            int It is used for:\n * <ul>\n *   <li>Parsing incoming produce requests from clients</li>\n *   <li>Reading/modifying batches in the log</li>\n *   <li>Filtering and compacting log segments</li>\n *   <li>Transmitting batches over the network</li>\n * </ul>\n *\n * <p><b>Memory Layout:</b> The buffer contains a sequence of concatenated batches. Each batch\n * begins with a base offset (8 bytes) followed by the batch length (4 bytes), allowing sequential\n * iteration. Use {@link #batchIterator()} to parse batches lazily without loading all data\n * into memory.\n *\n * <p><b>Thread Safety:</b> This class is not thread-safe. The underlying {@link ByteBuffer}\n * is not protected from concurrent access. Multiple threads must not access the same\n * {@code MemoryRecords} instance concurrently. Iterators and filtered results are also\n * not thread-safe.\n *\n * <p><b>Lazy Evaluation:</b> Batch parsing is performed lazily when batches are requested.\n * No validation or decompression occurs until {@link #batchIterator()}, {@link #batches()},\n * or {@link #filterTo(RecordFilter, ByteBuffer, BufferSupplier)} is called.\n *\n * <p><b>Buffer Ownership:</b> {@code MemoryRecords} does not take ownership of the backing\n * buffer. The caller is responsible for managing the buffer's lifecycle and ensuring it\n * remains valid while the {@code MemoryRecords} instance is in use.\n *\n * <p><b>Creating Records:</b> Use the factory methods {@link #builder(ByteBuffer, Compression, TimestampType, long)}\n * or {@link #withRecords(Compression, SimpleRecord...)} to create new batches. The buffer is temporarily marked and\n     * reset to preserve its state.\n     *\n     * @param channel The channel to write to\n     * @return The total number of bytes written\n     * @throws IOException For any IO errors writing to the channel\n     */\n    public int writeFullyTo(GatheringByteChannel channel) throws IOException {\n        buffer.mark();\n        int written = 0;\n        while (written < sizeInBytes())\n            written += channel.write(buffer);\n        buffer.reset();\n        return written;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * The total number of bytes in this message set not including any partial, trailing messages.\n     *\n     * <p>This may be smaller than what is returned by {@link #sizeInBytes()} if the buffer\n     * ends with an incomplete batch header. This method iterates all batches to compute the\n     * valid byte count and caches the result.\n     *\n     * @return The number of valid bytes\n     */\n    public int validBytes() {\n        if (validBytes >= 0)\n            return validBytes;\n\n        int bytes = 0;\n        for (RecordBatch batch : batches())\n            bytes += batch.sizeInBytes();\n\n        this.validBytes = bytes;\n        return bytes;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public AbstractIterator<MutableRecordBatch> batchIterator() {\n        return new RecordBatchIterator<>(new ByteBufferLogInputStream(buffer.duplicate(), Integer.MAX_VALUE));\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validates the header of the first batch and returns its size.\n     *\n     * <p>This method reads only the batch header (up to the magic byte and length field)\n     * without validating the full batch or decompressing records.\n     *\n     * @return First batch size including {@link Records#LOG_OVERHEAD} if buffer contains\n     *         header up to magic byte, {@code null} if insufficient data\n     * @throws CorruptRecordException if the record size or magic value is invalid\n     */\n    public Integer firstBatchSize() {\n        if (buffer.remaining() < HEADER_SIZE_UP_TO_MAGIC)\n            return null;\n        return new ByteBufferLogInputStream(buffer, Integer.MAX_VALUE).nextBatchSize();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Filter the records into the provided ByteBuffer.\n     *\n     * <p>This method processes each batch in the buffer, applying a user-provided filter to\n     * determine which records to retain. It handles:\n     * <ul>\n     *   <li>Batch-level filtering decisions (delete entire batch, retain if empty, etc.)</li>\n     *   <li>Record-level filtering within retained batches</li>\n     *   <li>Decompression and recompression of compressed batches</li>\n     *   <li>Empty batch retention for producer state preservation</li>\n     *   <li>Delete horizon markers for time-based retention</li>\n     * </ul>\n     *\n     * <p>The filter is called for each batch and potentially each record. Implementations\n     * should be efficient as they are called on every log compaction.\n     *\n     * @param filter The filter function that determines which batches and records to retain\n     * @param destinationBuffer The byte buffer to write the filtered records to. For small record batches, allocating a\n     *                                     potentially large buffer (64 KB for LZ4) will dominate\n     *                                     the cost of decompressing and iterating. A supplier\n     *                                     that reuses buffers will have significant performance\n     *                                     impact.\n     * @return A {@link FilterResult} decompressionBufferSupplier);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Note: This method is also used to convert the first timestamp of the batch (which is usually the timestamp of the first record)\n     * to the delete horizon of the tombstones or txn markers which are present in the batch.\n     */\n    private static FilterResult filterTo(Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches, RecordFilter filter,\n                                         ByteBuffer destinationBuffer, BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier) {\n        FilterResult filterResult = new FilterResult(destinationBuffer);\n        ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream = new ByteBufferOutputStream(destinationBuffer);\n        for (MutableRecordBatch batch : batches) {\n            final BatchRetentionResult batchRetentionResult = filter.checkBatchRetention(batch);\n            final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = batchRetentionResult.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            final BatchRetention batchRetention = batchRetentionResult.batchRetention;\n\n            filterResult.bytesRead += batch.sizeInBytes();\n\n            if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.DELETE)\n                continue;\n\n            final BatchFilterResult iterationResult = filterBatch(batch, decompressionBufferSupplier, filterResult,\n                filter);\n            List<Record> retainedRecords = iterationResult.retainedRecords;\n            boolean containsTombstones = iterationResult.containsTombstones;\n            boolean writeOriginalBatch = iterationResult.writeOriginalBatch;\n            long maxOffset = iterationResult.maxOffset;\n\n            if (!retainedRecords.isEmpty()) {\n                // we check if the delete horizon should be set to a new value\n                // in which case, we need to reset the base timestamp and overwrite the timestamp deltas\n                // if the batch does not contain tombstones, then we don't need to overwrite batch\n                boolean needToSetDeleteHorizon = (containsTombstones || containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) &&\n                    batch.deleteHorizonMs().isEmpty();\n                if (writeOriginalBatch && !needToSetDeleteHorizon) {\n                    batch.writeTo(bufferOutputStream);\n                    filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, retainedRecords.size(), false);\n                } else {\n                    long deleteHorizonMs;\n                    if (needToSetDeleteHorizon)\n                        deleteHorizonMs = filter.currentTime + filter.deleteRetentionMs;\n                    else\n                        deleteHorizonMs = batch.deleteHorizonMs().orElse(RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP);\n                    try (final MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(info.maxTimestamp, info.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp,\n                            maxOffset, retainedRecords.size(), filteredBatchSize);\n                    }\n                }\n            } else if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.RETAIN_EMPTY) {\n                if (batch.magic() < RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2) // should never happen\n                    throw new IllegalStateException(\"Empty batches are only supported for magic v2 and above\");\n\n                bufferOutputStream.ensureRemaining(DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD);\n                DefaultRecordBatch.writeEmptyHeader(bufferOutputStream.buffer(), RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, batch.producerId(),\n                        batch.producerEpoch(), batch.baseSequence(), batch.baseOffset(), batch.lastOffset(),\n                        batch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), batch.timestampType(), batch.maxTimestamp(),\n                        batch.isTransactional(), batch.isControlBatch());\n                filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, 0, true);\n            }\n\n            // If we had to allocate a new buffer to fit the filtered buffer (see KAFKA-5316), return early to\n            // avoid the need for additional allocations.\n            ByteBuffer outputBuffer = bufferOutputStream.buffer();\n            if (outputBuffer != destinationBuffer) {\n                filterResult.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\n                return filterResult;\n            }\n        }\n\n        return filterResult;\n    }\n\n    private static BatchFilterResult filterBatch(RecordBatch batch,\n                                                 BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier,\n                                                 FilterResult filterResult,\n                                                 RecordFilter filter) {\n        try (final CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = batch.streamingIterator(decompressionBufferSupplier)) {\n            long maxOffset = -1;\n            boolean containsTombstones = false;\n            // Convert records with old record versions\n            boolean writeOriginalBatch = batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE;\n            List<Record> retainedRecords = new ArrayList<>();\n            while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n                Record record = iterator.next();\n                filterResult.messagesRead += 1;\n\n                if (filter.shouldRetainRecord(batch, record)) {\n                    if (record.offset() > maxOffset)\n                        maxOffset = record.offset();\n\n                    retainedRecords.add(record);\n\n                    if (!record.hasValue()) {\n                        containsTombstones = true;\n                    }\n                } else {\n                    writeOriginalBatch = false;\n                }\n            }\n            return new BatchFilterResult(retainedRecords, writeOriginalBatch, containsTombstones, maxOffset);\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static class BatchFilterResult {\n        private final List<Record> retainedRecords;\n        private final boolean writeOriginalBatch;\n        private final boolean containsTombstones;\n        private final long maxOffset;\n        private BatchFilterResult(List<Record> retainedRecords,\n                                  final boolean writeOriginalBatch,\n                                  final boolean containsTombstones,\n                                  final long maxOffset) {\n            this.retainedRecords = retainedRecords;\n            this.writeOriginalBatch = writeOriginalBatch;\n            this.containsTombstones = containsTombstones;\n            this.maxOffset = maxOffset;\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static MemoryRecordsBuilder buildRetainedRecordsInto(RecordBatch originalBatch,\n                                                                 List<Record> retainedRecords,\n                                                                 ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream,\n                                                                 final long deleteHorizonMs) {\n        Compression compression = Compression.of(originalBatch.compressionType()).build();\n        // V0 has no timestamp type or timestamp, so we set the timestamp to CREATE_TIME and timestamp to NO_TIMESTAMP.\n        // Note that this differs from produce up-conversion where the timestamp type topic config is used and the log append\n        // time is generated if the config is LOG_APPEND_TIME. The reason for the different behavior is that there is\n        // no appropriate log append time we can generate at compaction time.\n        TimestampType timestampType = originalBatch.timestampType() == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE ?\n                TimestampType.CREATE_TIME : originalBatch.timestampType();\n        long logAppendTime = timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME ?\n                originalBatch.maxTimestamp() : RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        long baseOffset = originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 ?\n                originalBatch.baseOffset() : retainedRecords.get(0).offset();\n\n        // Convert records with older record versions to the current one\n        MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(bufferOutputStream, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE,\n                compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime, originalBatch.producerId(),\n                originalBatch.producerEpoch(), originalBatch.baseSequence(), originalBatch.isTransactional(),\n                originalBatch.isControlBatch(), originalBatch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), bufferOutputStream.limit(), deleteHorizonMs);\n\n        for (Record record : retainedRecords)\n            builder.append(record);\n\n        if (originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2)\n            // we must preserve the last offset from the initial batch in order to ensure that the\n            // last sequence number from the batch remains even after compaction. Otherwise, the producer\n            // could incorrectly see an out of sequence error.\n            builder.overrideLastOffset(originalBatch.lastOffset());\n\n        return builder;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get the byte buffer that backs this instance for reading.\n     *\n     * <p>Returns a duplicate of the backing buffer, so modifications to the returned buffer's\n     * position or limit will not affect this instance, but modifications to the buffer's\n     * contents will be visible.\n     *\n     * @return A duplicate of the backing buffer\n     */\n    public ByteBuffer buffer() {\n        return buffer.duplicate();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public MemoryRecords slice(int position, int size) {\n        if (position < 0)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid position: \" + position + \" in read from \" + this);\n        if (position > buffer.limit())\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Slice from position \" + position + \" exceeds end position of \" + this);\n        if (size < 0)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid size: \" + size + \" in read from \" + this);\n\n        int availableBytes = Math.min(size, buffer.limit() - position);\n        // As of now, clients module support Java11 hence can't use ByteBuffer::slice(position, size) method.\n        // So we need to create a duplicate buffer and set the position and limit. Duplicate buffer\n        // is backed by original bytes hence not the content but only the relative position and limit\n        // are changed in the duplicate buffer. Once the position and limit are set, we can call the\n        // slice method to get the sliced buffer, which is a backed by the original buffer with the\n        // position reset to 0 and limit set to the size of the slice.\n        ByteBuffer slicedBuffer = buffer.duplicate();\n        slicedBuffer.position(position);\n        slicedBuffer.limit(position + availableBytes);\n        // Reset the position to 0 so that the sliced view has a relative position.\n        slicedBuffer = slicedBuffer.slice();\n\n        return readableRecords(slicedBuffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches() {\n        return batches;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"MemoryRecords(size=\" + sizeInBytes() +\n                \", buffer=\" + buffer +\n                \")\";\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean equals(Object o) {\n        if (this == o)\n            return true;\n        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass())\n            return false;\n\n        MemoryRecords that = (MemoryRecords) o;\n\n        return buffer.equals(that.buffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int hashCode() {\n        return buffer.hashCode();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Abstract base class for record filtering during log compaction and retention.\n     *\n     * <p>Subclasses implement batch-level and record-level filtering decisions. Filters are\n     * applied in two phases:\n     * <ol>\n     *   <li>Batch-level decision via {@link #checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch)}</li>\n     *   <li>Record-level decision via {@link #shouldRetainRecord(RecordBatch, Record)}</li>\n     * </ol>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Thread Safety:</b> Filter implementations are not thread-safe. Used to calculate delete horizon\n         * timestamps for tombstones and transaction markers.\n         */\n        public final long deleteRetentionMs;\n\n        /**\n         * Create a {@code RecordFilter} with the given parameters.\n         *\n         * @param currentTime The current time in milliseconds\n         * @param deleteRetentionMs The delete retention time in milliseconds\n         */\n        public RecordFilter(final long currentTime, final long deleteRetentionMs) {\n            this.currentTime = currentTime;\n            this.deleteRetentionMs = deleteRetentionMs;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Result of a batch-level retention check.\n         */\n        public static class BatchRetentionResult {\n            /**\n             * The batch retention decision.\n             */\n            public final BatchRetention batchRetention;\n\n            /**\n             * Whether the batch contains an empty transaction marker.\n             */\n            public final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n\n            /**\n             * Create a {@code BatchRetentionResult}.\n             *\n             * @param batchRetention The retention decision\n             * @param containsMarkerForEmptyTxn Whether the batch contains an empty txn marker\n             */\n            public BatchRetentionResult(final BatchRetention batchRetention,\n                                        final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) {\n                this.batchRetention = batchRetention;\n                this.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            }\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Batch retention decisions.\n         */\n        public enum BatchRetention {\n            /**\n             * Delete the entire batch without inspecting individual records.\n             */\n            DELETE,\n\n            /**\n             * Retain the batch even if it becomes empty after record filtering.\n             */\n            RETAIN_EMPTY,\n\n            /**\n             * Delete the batch only if it is empty after record filtering.\n             */\n            DELETE_EMPTY\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Check whether the full batch can be discarded (i.e. whether we even need to\n         * check the records individually).\n         *\n         * <p>This method is called first for each batch. If it returns {@link BatchRetention#DELETE},\n         * the batch is skipped entirely and {@link #shouldRetainRecord(RecordBatch, Record)}\n         * is not called for any records in this batch.\n         *\n         * @param batch The batch to check\n         * @return A {@code BatchRetentionResult} with the retention decision and transaction marker info\n         */\n        protected abstract BatchRetentionResult checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch batch);\n\n        /**\n         * Check whether a record should be retained in the log.\n         *\n         * <p>This method is called for each record in batches that were not explicitly\n         * discarded with {@link BatchRetention#DELETE}.\n         *\n         * <p>Note that {@link #checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch)} is used prior to checking\n         * individual record retention.\n         *\n         * @param recordBatch The batch containing the record\n         * @param record The record to check\n         * @return {@code true} if the record should be retained, {@code false} otherwise\n         */\n        protected abstract boolean shouldRetainRecord(RecordBatch recordBatch, Record record);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Summary of a filtering operation.\n     *\n     * <p>This class provides metrics about which records/batches were processed and retained\n     * during filtering. It is used for logging and monitoring compaction progress.\n     */\n    public static class FilterResult {\n        /**\n         * The output buffer containing filtered records.\n         */\n        private ByteBuffer outputBuffer;\n\n        /**\n         * The number of records/messages read from all batches.\n         */\n        private int messagesRead = 0;\n\n        /**\n         * The total bytes read (including from discarded batches).\n         */\n        private int bytesRead = 0;\n\n        /**\n         * The number of records retained after filtering.\n         */\n        private int messagesRetained = 0;\n\n        /**\n         * The total bytes retained after filtering.\n         */\n        private int bytesRetained = 0;\n\n        /**\n         * The maximum offset across all retained records.\n         */\n        private long maxOffset = -1L;\n\n        /**\n         * The maximum timestamp across all retained records.\n         */\n        private long maxTimestamp = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n\n        /**\n         * The offset of the record with the maximum timestamp (shallow offset, pre-compaction).\n         */\n        private long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = -1L;\n\n        private FilterResult(ByteBuffer outputBuffer) {\n            this.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\n        }\n\n        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(MutableRecordBatch retainedBatch, int numMessagesInBatch, boolean headerOnly) {\n            int bytesRetained = headerOnly ? DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD : retainedBatch.sizeInBytes();\n            updateRetainedBatchMetadata(retainedBatch.maxTimestamp(), retainedBatch.lastOffset(),\n                    retainedBatch.lastOffset(), numMessagesInBatch, bytesRetained);\n        }\n\n        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset,\n                                                 int messagesRetained, int bytesRetained) {\n            validateBatchMetadata(maxTimestamp, shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, maxOffset);\n            if (maxTimestamp > this.maxTimestamp) {\n                this.maxTimestamp = maxTimestamp;\n                this.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp;\n            }\n            this.maxOffset = Math.max(maxOffset, this.maxOffset);\n            this.messagesRetained += messagesRetained;\n            this.bytesRetained += bytesRetained;\n        }\n\n        private void validateBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset) {\n            if (maxTimestamp != RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP && shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp < 0)\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"shallowOffset undefined for maximum timestamp \" + maxTimestamp);\n            if (maxOffset < 0)\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"maxOffset undefined\");\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the output buffer containing filtered records.\n         *\n         * @return The output buffer\n         */\n        public ByteBuffer outputBuffer() {\n            return outputBuffer;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the total number of messages read during filtering.\n         *\n         * @return The number of messages read\n         */\n        public int messagesRead() {\n            return messagesRead;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the total bytes read during filtering (including discarded batches).\n         *\n         * @return The number of bytes read\n         */\n        public int bytesRead() {\n            return bytesRead;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the total number of messages retained after filtering.\n         *\n         * @return The number of messages retained\n         */\n        public int messagesRetained() {\n            return messagesRetained;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the total bytes retained after filtering.\n         *\n         * @return The number of bytes retained\n         */\n        public int bytesRetained() {\n            return bytesRetained;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the maximum offset of retained records.\n         *\n         * @return The maximum offset, or -1L if no records were retained\n         */\n        public long maxOffset() {\n            return maxOffset;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the maximum timestamp of retained records.\n         *\n         * @return The maximum timestamp\n         */\n        public long maxTimestamp() {\n            return maxTimestamp;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the shallow offset of the record with the maximum timestamp.\n         *\n         * @return The shallow offset of max timestamp record, or -1L if not set\n         */\n        public long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp() {\n            return shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new {@code MemoryRecords} instance backed by the given buffer for reading.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to back the instance. Cannot be null.\n     * @return A new {@code MemoryRecords} instance\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords readableRecords(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        return new MemoryRecords(buffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for the given buffer.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write records to\n     * @param compression The compression type to timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset) {\n        return builder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, timestampType, baseOffset);\n    }\n\n parameters including producer information.\n     *\n     * @param magic The magic version\n     * @param initialOffset The base offset for records\n     * @param compression The compression type to use\n     * @param timestampType The timestamp type\n     * @param producerId The producer ID\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer epoch\n     * @param baseSequence The base sequence number\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param isTransactional Whether records are transactional\n     * @param records The records to include\n     * @return {@code MemoryRecords} containing the records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withRecords(byte magic, long initialOffset, Compression compression,\n                                            TimestampType timestampType, long producerId, short producerEpoch,\n                                            int baseSequence, int partitionLeaderEpoch, boolean isTransactional,\n                                            SimpleRecord... records) {\n        if (records.length == 0)\n            return MemoryRecords.EMPTY;\n        int sizeEstimate = AbstractRecords.estimateSizeInBytes(magic, compression.type(), Arrays.asList(records));\n        ByteBufferOutputStream bufferStream = new ByteBufferOutputStream(sizeEstimate);\n        long logAppendTime = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            logAppendTime = System.currentTimeMillis();\n        try (final MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(bufferStream, magic, compression, timestampType,\n                initialOffset, logAppendTime, producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional, false,\n                partitionLeaderEpoch, sizeEstimate)) {\n            for (SimpleRecord record : records)\n                builder.append(record);\n            return builder.build();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create {@code MemoryRecords} with MemoryRecords} containing the marker\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withEndTransactionMarker(long producerId, short producerEpoch, EndTransactionMarker marker) {\n        return withEndTransactionMarker(0L, System.currentTimeMillis(), RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH,\n                producerId, producerEpoch, marker);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create {@code MemoryRecords} with end transaction marker and timestamp.\n     *\n     * @param timestamp The timestamp for the marker\n     * @param producerId The producer ID\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer epoch\n     * @param marker The end transaction marker\n     * @return {@code MemoryRecords} containing the marker\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withEndTransactionMarker(long timestamp, long producerId, short producerEpoch,\n                                                         EndTransactionMarker marker) {\n        return withEndTransactionMarker(0L, timestamp,  *\n     * @param initialOffset The base offset\n     * @param timestamp The timestamp for the marker\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param producerId The producer ID\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer epoch\n     * @param marker The end transaction marker\n     * @return {@code MemoryRecords} containing the marker\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withEndTransactionMarker(long initialOffset, long timestamp, int partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                                                         long producerId, short producerEpoch,\n                                                         EndTransactionMarker marker) {\n        int endTxnMarkerBatchSize = DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD + marker.endTxnMarkerValueSize();\n        ByteBuffer buffer = ByteBuffer.allocate(endTxnMarkerBatchSize);\n        writeEndTransactionalMarker(buffer, initialOffset, timestamp, partitionLeaderEpoch, producerId,\n                producerEpoch, marker);\n        buffer.flip();\n        return MemoryRecords.readableRecords(buffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write an end transaction marker to a buffer.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param initialOffset The base offset\n     * @param timestamp The timestamp for the marker\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param producerId The producer ID\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer epoch\n     * @param marker The end transaction marker\n     */\n    public static void writeEndTransactionalMarker(ByteBuffer buffer, long initialOffset, long timestamp,\n                                                   int partitionLeaderEpoch, long producerId, short producerEpoch,\n                                                   EndTransactionMarker marker) {\n        boolean isTransactional = true;\n        try (MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(buffer, It is used for:\n * <ul>\n *   <li>Parsing incoming produce requests from clients</li>\n *   <li>Reading/modifying batches in the log</li>\n *   <li>Filtering and compacting log segments</li>\n *   <li>Transmitting batches over the network</li>\n * </ul>\n *\n * <p><b>Memory Layout:</b> The buffer contains a sequence of concatenated batches. Each batch\n * begins with a base offset (8 bytes) followed by the batch length (4 bytes), allowing sequential\n * iteration. Use {@link #batchIterator()} to parse batches lazily without loading all data\n * into memory.\n *\n * <p><b>Thread Safety:</b> This class is not thread-safe. The underlying {@link ByteBuffer}\n * is not protected from concurrent access. Multiple threads must not access the same\n * {@code MemoryRecords} instance concurrently. Iterators and filtered results are also\n * not thread-safe.\n *\n * <p><b>Lazy Evaluation:</b> Batch parsing is performed lazily when batches are requested.\n * No validation or decompression occurs until {@link #batchIterator()}, {@link #batches()},\n * or {@link #filterTo(RecordFilter, ByteBuffer, BufferSupplier)} is called.\n *\n * <p><b>Buffer Ownership:</b> {@code MemoryRecords} does not take ownership of the backing\n * buffer. The caller is responsible for managing the buffer's lifecycle and ensuring it\n * remains valid while the {@code MemoryRecords} instance is in use.\n *\n * <p><b>Creating Records:</b> Use the factory methods {@link #builder(ByteBuffer, Compression, TimestampType, long)}\n * or {@link #withRecords(Compression, SimpleRecord...)} to create new batches. These return\n * a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for efficient batch construction.\n *\n * <p><b>Filtering and Compaction:</b> The {@link #filterTo(RecordFilter, ByteBuffer, BufferSupplier)}\n * method supports log compaction and retention filtering. It handles compressed batches,\n * empty batches, and delete horizon markers. Filters can specify batch-level retention\n * decisions or examine individual records.\n *\n * @see RecordBatch\n * @see DefaultRecordBatch\n * @see MemoryRecordsBuilder\n * @see Records\n */\npublic class MemoryRecords extends AbstractRecords {\n    /**\n     * An empty {@code MemoryRecords} instance backed by an empty buffer.\n     */\n    public static final MemoryRecords EMPTY = MemoryRecords.readableRecords(ByteBuffer.allocate(0));\n\n    private final ByteBuffer buffer;\n\n    private final Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches = this::batchIterator;\n\n    private int validBytes = -1;\n\n    // Construct a writable memory records\n    /**\n     * Create a {@code MemoryRecords} instance backed by the given buffer.\n     *\n     * <p>The buffer must contain valid record batch data (or be empty). The buffer's position,\n     * limit, and content must not be modified externally while this instance is in use.\n     *\n     * @param buffer A {@link ByteBuffer} containing serialized record batches. Cannot be null.\n     * @throws NullPointerException if buffer is null\n     */\n    private MemoryRecords(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        Objects.requireNonNull(buffer, \"buffer should not be null\");\n        this.buffer = buffer;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int sizeInBytes() {\n        return buffer.limit();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int writeTo(TransferableChannel channel, int position, int length) throws IOException {\n        if (((long) position) + length > buffer.limit())\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"position+length should not be greater than buffer.limit(), position: \"\n                    + position + \", length: \" + length + \", buffer.limit(): \" + buffer.limit());\n\n        return Utils.tryWriteTo(channel, position, length, buffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write all records to the given channel (including partial records).\n     *\n     * <p>This method writes the entire buffer to the channel, potentially in multiple writes\n     * if the channel cannot accept all data at once. The buffer is temporarily marked and\n     * reset to preserve its state.\n     *\n     * @param channel The channel to write to\n     * @return The total number of bytes written\n     * @throws IOException For any IO errors writing to the channel\n     */\n    public int writeFullyTo(GatheringByteChannel channel) throws IOException {\n        buffer.mark();\n        int written = 0;\n        while (written < sizeInBytes())\n            written += channel.write(buffer);\n        buffer.reset();\n        return written;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * The total number of bytes in this message set not including any partial, trailing messages.\n     *\n     * <p>This may be smaller than what is returned by {@link #sizeInBytes()} if the buffer\n     * ends with an incomplete batch header. This method iterates all batches to compute the\n     * valid byte count and caches the result.\n     *\n     * @return The number of valid bytes\n     */\n    public int validBytes() {\n        if (validBytes >= 0)\n            return validBytes;\n\n        int bytes = 0;\n        for (RecordBatch batch : batches())\n            bytes += batch.sizeInBytes();\n\n        this.validBytes = bytes;\n        return bytes;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public AbstractIterator<MutableRecordBatch> batchIterator() {\n        return new RecordBatchIterator<>(new ByteBufferLogInputStream(buffer.duplicate(), Integer.MAX_VALUE));\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validates the header of the first batch and returns its size.\n     *\n     * <p>This method reads only the batch header (up to the magic byte and length field)\n     * without validating the full batch or decompressing records.\n     *\n     * @return First batch size including {@link Records#LOG_OVERHEAD} if buffer contains\n     *         header up to magic byte, {@code null} if insufficient data\n     * @throws CorruptRecordException if the record size or magic value is invalid\n     */\n    public Integer firstBatchSize() {\n        if (buffer.remaining() < HEADER_SIZE_UP_TO_MAGIC)\n            return null;\n        return new ByteBufferLogInputStream(buffer, Integer.MAX_VALUE).nextBatchSize();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Filter the records into the provided ByteBuffer.\n     *\n     * <p>This method processes each batch in the buffer, applying a user-provided filter to\n     * determine which records to retain. It handles:\n     * <ul>\n     *   <li>Batch-level filtering decisions (delete entire batch, retain if empty, etc.)</li>\n     *   <li>Record-level filtering within retained batches</li>\n     *   <li>Decompression and recompression of compressed batches</li>\n     *   <li>Empty batch retention for producer state preservation</li>\n     *   <li>Delete horizon markers for time-based retention</li>\n     * </ul>\n     *\n     * <p>The filter is called for each batch and potentially each record. Implementations\n     * should be efficient as they are called on every log compaction.\n     *\n     * @param filter The filter function that determines which batches and records to retain\n     * @param destinationBuffer The byte buffer to write the filtered records to. Must have\n     *                           sufficient capacity or be resizable.\n     * @param decompressionBufferSupplier The supplier of ByteBuffer(s) used for decompression\n     *                                     if supported. For small record batches, allocating a\n     *                                     potentially large buffer (64 KB for LZ4) will dominate\n     *                                     the cost of decompressing and iterating. A supplier\n     *                                     that reuses buffers will have significant performance\n     *                                     impact.\n     * @return A {@link FilterResult} with a summary of the output (for metrics) and potentially\n     *         an overflow buffer if the destination was too small\n     * @see RecordFilter\n     * @see FilterResult\n     */\n    public FilterResult filterTo(RecordFilter filter, ByteBuffer destinationBuffer, BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier) {\n        return filterTo(batches(), filter, destinationBuffer, decompressionBufferSupplier);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Note: This method is also used to convert the first timestamp of the batch (which is usually the timestamp of the first record)\n     * to the delete horizon of the tombstones or txn markers which are present in the batch.\n     */\n    private static FilterResult filterTo(Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches, RecordFilter filter,\n                                         ByteBuffer destinationBuffer, BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier) {\n        FilterResult filterResult = new FilterResult(destinationBuffer);\n        ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream = new ByteBufferOutputStream(destinationBuffer);\n        for (MutableRecordBatch batch : batches) {\n            final BatchRetentionResult batchRetentionResult = filter.checkBatchRetention(batch);\n            final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = batchRetentionResult.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            final BatchRetention batchRetention = batchRetentionResult.batchRetention;\n\n            filterResult.bytesRead += batch.sizeInBytes();\n\n            if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.DELETE)\n                continue;\n\n            final BatchFilterResult iterationResult = filterBatch(batch, decompressionBufferSupplier, filterResult,\n                filter);\n            List<Record> retainedRecords = iterationResult.retainedRecords;\n            boolean containsTombstones = iterationResult.containsTombstones;\n            boolean writeOriginalBatch = iterationResult.writeOriginalBatch;\n            long maxOffset = iterationResult.maxOffset;\n\n            if (!retainedRecords.isEmpty()) {\n                // we check if the delete horizon should be set to a new value\n                // in which case, we need to reset the base timestamp and overwrite the timestamp deltas\n                // if the batch does not contain tombstones, then we don't need to overwrite batch\n                boolean needToSetDeleteHorizon = (containsTombstones || containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) &&\n                    batch.deleteHorizonMs().isEmpty();\n                if (writeOriginalBatch && !needToSetDeleteHorizon) {\n                    batch.writeTo(bufferOutputStream);\n                    filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, retainedRecords.size(), false);\n                } else {\n                    long deleteHorizonMs;\n                    if (needToSetDeleteHorizon)\n                        deleteHorizonMs = filter.currentTime + filter.deleteRetentionMs;\n                    else\n                        deleteHorizonMs = batch.deleteHorizonMs().orElse(RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP);\n                    try (final MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = buildRetainedRecordsInto(batch, retainedRecords,\n                            bufferOutputStream, deleteHorizonMs)) {\n                        MemoryRecords records = builder.build();\n                        int filteredBatchSize = records.sizeInBytes();\n                        MemoryRecordsBuilder.RecordsInfo info = builder.info();\n                        filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(info.maxTimestamp, info.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp,\n                            maxOffset, retainedRecords.size(), filteredBatchSize);\n                    }\n                }\n            } else if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.RETAIN_EMPTY) {\n                if (batch.magic() < RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2) // should never happen\n                    throw new IllegalStateException(\"Empty batches are only supported for magic v2 and above\");\n\n                bufferOutputStream.ensureRemaining(DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD);\n                DefaultRecordBatch.writeEmptyHeader(bufferOutputStream.buffer(), RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, batch.producerId(),\n                        batch.producerEpoch(), batch.baseSequence(), batch.baseOffset(), batch.lastOffset(),\n                        batch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), batch.timestampType(), batch.maxTimestamp(),\n                        batch.isTransactional(), batch.isControlBatch());\n                filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, 0, true);\n            }\n\n            // If we had to allocate a new buffer to fit the filtered buffer (see KAFKA-5316), return early to\n            // avoid the need for additional allocations.\n            ByteBuffer outputBuffer = bufferOutputStream.buffer();\n            if (outputBuffer != destinationBuffer) {\n                filterResult.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\n                return filterResult;\n            }\n        }\n\n        return filterResult;\n    }\n\n    private static BatchFilterResult filterBatch(RecordBatch batch,\n                                                 BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier,\n                                                 FilterResult filterResult,\n                                                 RecordFilter filter) {\n        try (final CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = batch.streamingIterator(decompressionBufferSupplier)) {\n            long maxOffset = -1;\n            boolean containsTombstones = false;\n            // Convert records with old record versions\n            boolean writeOriginalBatch = batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE;\n            List<Record> retainedRecords = new ArrayList<>();\n            while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n                Record record = iterator.next();\n                filterResult.messagesRead += 1;\n\n                if (filter.shouldRetainRecord(batch, record)) {\n                    if (record.offset() > maxOffset)\n                        maxOffset = record.offset();\n\n                    retainedRecords.add(record);\n\n                    if (!record.hasValue()) {\n                        containsTombstones = true;\n                    }\n                } else {\n                    writeOriginalBatch = false;\n                }\n            }\n            return new BatchFilterResult(retainedRecords, writeOriginalBatch, containsTombstones, maxOffset);\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static class BatchFilterResult {\n        private final List<Record> retainedRecords;\n        private final boolean writeOriginalBatch;\n        private final boolean containsTombstones;\n        private final long maxOffset;\n        private BatchFilterResult(List<Record> retainedRecords,\n                                  final boolean writeOriginalBatch,\n                                  final boolean containsTombstones,\n                                  final long maxOffset) {\n            this.retainedRecords = retainedRecords;\n            this.writeOriginalBatch = writeOriginalBatch;\n            this.containsTombstones = containsTombstones;\n            this.maxOffset = maxOffset;\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static MemoryRecordsBuilder buildRetainedRecordsInto(RecordBatch originalBatch,\n                                                                 List<Record> retainedRecords,\n                                                                 ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream,\n                                                                 final long deleteHorizonMs) {\n        Compression compression = Compression.of(originalBatch.compressionType()).build();\n        // V0 has no timestamp type or timestamp, so we set the timestamp to CREATE_TIME and timestamp to NO_TIMESTAMP.\n        // Note that this differs from produce up-conversion where the timestamp type topic config is used and the log append\n        // time is generated if the config is LOG_APPEND_TIME. The reason for the different behavior is that there is\n        // no appropriate log append time we can generate at compaction time.\n        TimestampType timestampType = originalBatch.timestampType() == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE ?\n                TimestampType.CREATE_TIME : originalBatch.timestampType();\n        long logAppendTime = timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME ?\n                originalBatch.maxTimestamp() : RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        long baseOffset = originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 ?\n                originalBatch.baseOffset() : retainedRecords.get(0).offset();\n\n        // Convert records with older record versions to the current one\n        MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(bufferOutputStream, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE,\n                compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime, originalBatch.producerId(),\n                originalBatch.producerEpoch(), originalBatch.baseSequence(), originalBatch.isTransactional(),\n                originalBatch.isControlBatch(), originalBatch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), bufferOutputStream.limit(), deleteHorizonMs);\n\n        for (Record record : retainedRecords)\n            builder.append(record);\n\n        if (originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2)\n            // we must preserve the last offset from the initial batch in order to ensure that the\n            // last sequence number from the batch remains even after compaction. Otherwise, the producer\n            // could incorrectly see an out of sequence error.\n            builder.overrideLastOffset(originalBatch.lastOffset());\n\n        return builder;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get the byte buffer that backs this instance for reading.\n     *\n     * <p>Returns a duplicate of the backing buffer, so modifications to the returned buffer's\n     * position or limit will not affect this instance, but modifications to the buffer's\n     * contents will be visible.\n     *\n     * @return A duplicate of the backing buffer\n     */\n    public ByteBuffer buffer() {\n        return buffer.duplicate();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public MemoryRecords slice(int position, int size) {\n        if (position < 0)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid position: \" + position + \" in read from \" + this);\n        if (position > buffer.limit())\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Slice from position \" + position + \" exceeds end position of \" + this);\n        if (size < 0)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid size: \" + size + \" in read from \" + this);\n\n        int availableBytes = Math.min(size, buffer.limit() - position);\n        // As of now, clients module support Java11 hence can't use ByteBuffer::slice(position, size) method.\n        // So we need to create a duplicate buffer and set the position and limit. Duplicate buffer\n        // is backed by original bytes hence not the content but only the relative position and limit\n        // are changed in the duplicate buffer. Once the position and limit are set, we can call the\n        // slice method to get the sliced buffer, which is a backed by the original buffer with the\n        // position reset to 0 and limit set to the size of the slice.\n        ByteBuffer slicedBuffer = buffer.duplicate();\n        slicedBuffer.position(position);\n        slicedBuffer.limit(position + availableBytes);\n        // Reset the position to 0 so that the sliced view has a relative position.\n        slicedBuffer = slicedBuffer.slice();\n\n        return readableRecords(slicedBuffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches() {\n        return batches;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"MemoryRecords(size=\" + sizeInBytes() +\n                \", buffer=\" + buffer +\n                \")\";\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean equals(Object o) {\n        if (this == o)\n            return true;\n        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass())\n            return false;\n\n        MemoryRecords that = (MemoryRecords) o;\n\n        return buffer.equals(that.buffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int hashCode() {\n        return buffer.hashCode();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Abstract base class for record filtering during log compaction and retention.\n     *\n     * <p>Subclasses implement batch-level and record-level filtering decisions. Filters are\n     * applied in two phases:\n     * <ol>\n     *   <li>Batch-level decision via {@link #checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch)}</li>\n     *   <li>Record-level decision via {@link #shouldRetainRecord(RecordBatch, Record)}</li>\n     * </ol>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Thread Safety:</b> Filter implementations are not thread-safe. A single filter\n     * instance should not be used from multiple threads concurrently.\n     *\n     * @see BatchRetention\n     */\n    public abstract static class RecordFilter {\n        /**\n         * The current time in milliseconds, used for time-based retention decisions.\n         */\n        public final long currentTime;\n\n        /**\n         * The delete retention time in milliseconds. Used to calculate delete horizon\n         * timestamps for tombstones and transaction markers.\n         */\n        public final long deleteRetentionMs;\n\n        /**\n         * Create a {@code RecordFilter} with the given parameters.\n         *\n         * @param currentTime The current time in milliseconds\n         * @param deleteRetentionMs The delete retention time in milliseconds\n         */\n        public RecordFilter(final long currentTime, final long deleteRetentionMs) {\n            this.currentTime = currentTime;\n            this.deleteRetentionMs = deleteRetentionMs;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Result of a batch-level retention check.\n         */\n        public static class BatchRetentionResult {\n            /**\n             * The batch retention decision.\n             */\n            public final BatchRetention batchRetention;\n\n            /**\n             * Whether the batch contains an empty transaction marker.\n             */\n            public final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n\n            /**\n             * Create a {@code BatchRetentionResult}.\n             *\n             * @param batchRetention The retention decision\n             * @param containsMarkerForEmptyTxn Whether the batch contains an empty txn marker\n             */\n            public BatchRetentionResult(final BatchRetention batchRetention,\n                                        final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) {\n                this.batchRetention = batchRetention;\n                this.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            }\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Batch retention decisions.\n         */\n        public enum BatchRetention {\n            /**\n             * Delete the entire batch without inspecting individual records.\n             */\n            DELETE,\n\n            /**\n             * Retain the batch even if it becomes empty after record filtering.\n             */\n            RETAIN_EMPTY,\n\n            /**\n             * Delete the batch only if it is empty after record filtering.\n             */\n            DELETE_EMPTY\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Check whether the full batch can be discarded (i.e. whether we even need to\n         * check the records individually).\n         *\n         * <p>This method is called first for each batch. If it returns {@link BatchRetention#DELETE},\n         * the batch is skipped entirely and {@link #shouldRetainRecord(RecordBatch, Record)}\n         * is not called for any records in this batch.\n         *\n         * @param batch The batch to check\n         * @return A {@code BatchRetentionResult} with the retention decision and transaction marker info\n         */\n        protected abstract BatchRetentionResult checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch batch);\n\n        /**\n         * Check whether a record should be retained in the log.\n         *\n         * <p>This method is called for each record in batches that were not explicitly\n         * discarded with {@link BatchRetention#DELETE}.\n         *\n         * <p>Note that {@link #checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch)} is used prior to checking\n         * individual record retention.\n         *\n         * @param recordBatch The batch containing the record\n         * @param record The record to check\n         * @return {@code true} if the record should be retained, {@code false} otherwise\n         */\n        protected abstract boolean shouldRetainRecord(RecordBatch recordBatch, Record record);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Summary of a filtering operation.\n     *\n     * <p>This class provides metrics about which records/batches were processed and retained\n     * during filtering. It is used for logging and monitoring compaction progress.\n     */\n    public static class FilterResult {\n        /**\n         * The output buffer containing filtered records.\n         */\n        private ByteBuffer outputBuffer;\n\n        /**\n         * The number of records/messages read from all batches.\n         */\n        private int messagesRead = 0;\n\n        /**\n         * The total bytes read (including from discarded batches).\n         */\n        private int bytesRead = 0;\n\n        /**\n         * The number of records retained after filtering.\n         */\n        private int messagesRetained = 0;\n\n        /**\n         * The total bytes retained after filtering.\n         */\n        private int bytesRetained = 0;\n\n        /**\n         * The maximum offset across all retained records.\n         */\n        private long maxOffset = -1L;\n\n        /**\n         * The maximum timestamp across all retained records.\n         */\n        private long maxTimestamp = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n\n        /**\n         * The offset of the record with the maximum timestamp (shallow offset, pre-compaction).\n         */\n        private long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = -1L;\n\n        private FilterResult(ByteBuffer outputBuffer) {\n            this.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\n        }\n\n        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(MutableRecordBatch retainedBatch, int numMessagesInBatch, boolean headerOnly) {\n            int bytesRetained = headerOnly ? DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD : retainedBatch.sizeInBytes();\n            updateRetainedBatchMetadata(retainedBatch.maxTimestamp(), retainedBatch.lastOffset(),\n                    retainedBatch.lastOffset(), numMessagesInBatch, bytesRetained);\n        }\n\n        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset,\n                                                 int messagesRetained, int bytesRetained) {\n            validateBatchMetadata(maxTimestamp, shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, maxOffset);\n            if (maxTimestamp > this.maxTimestamp) {\n                this.maxTimestamp = maxTimestamp;\n                this.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp;\n            }\n            this.maxOffset = Math.max(maxOffset, this.maxOffset);\n            this.messagesRetained += messagesRetained;\n            this.bytesRetained += bytesRetained;\n        }\n\n        private void validateBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset) {\n            if (maxTimestamp != RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP && shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp < 0)\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"shallowOffset undefined for maximum timestamp \" + maxTimestamp);\n            if (maxOffset < 0)\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"maxOffset undefined\");\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the output buffer containing filtered records.\n         *\n         * @return The output buffer\n         */\n        public ByteBuffer outputBuffer() {\n            return outputBuffer;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the total number of messages read during filtering.\n         *\n         * @return The number of messages read\n         */\n        public int messagesRead() {\n            return messagesRead;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the total bytes read during filtering (including discarded batches).\n         *\n         * @return The number of bytes read\n         */\n        public int bytesRead() {\n            return bytesRead;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the total number of messages retained after filtering.\n         *\n         * @return The number of messages retained\n         */\n        public int messagesRetained() {\n            return messagesRetained;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the total bytes retained after filtering.\n         *\n         * @return The number of bytes retained\n         */\n        public int bytesRetained() {\n            return bytesRetained;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the maximum offset of retained records.\n         *\n         * @return The maximum offset, or -1L if no records were retained\n         */\n        public long maxOffset() {\n            return maxOffset;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the maximum timestamp of retained records.\n         *\n         * @return The maximum timestamp\n         */\n        public long maxTimestamp() {\n            return maxTimestamp;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the shallow offset of the record with the maximum timestamp.\n         *\n         * @return The shallow offset of max timestamp record, or -1L if not set\n         */\n        public long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp() {\n            return shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new {@code MemoryRecords} instance backed by the given buffer for reading.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to back the instance. Cannot be null.\n     * @return A new {@code MemoryRecords} instance\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords readableRecords(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        return new MemoryRecords(buffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for the given buffer.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write records to\n     * @param compression The compression type to static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset) {\n        return builder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, timestampType, baseOffset);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} with a maximum size constraint.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write records to\n     * @param compression The compression type to false, false, RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH, maxSize);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} with magic version and log append time.\n     *\n     * @param buffer parameters including producer information.\n     *\n     * @param magic The magic version\n     * @param initialOffset The base offset for records\n     * @param compression The compression type to use\n     * @param timestampType The timestamp type\n     * @param producerId The producer ID\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer epoch\n     * @param baseSequence The base sequence number\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param isTransactional Whether records are transactional\n     * @param records The records to include\n     * @return {@code MemoryRecords} containing the records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withRecords(byte magic, long initialOffset, Compression compression,\n                                            TimestampType timestampType, long producerId, short producerEpoch,\n                                            int baseSequence, int partitionLeaderEpoch, boolean isTransactional,\n                                            SimpleRecord... records) {\n        if (records.length == 0)\n            return MemoryRecords.EMPTY;\n        int sizeEstimate = AbstractRecords.estimateSizeInBytes(magic, compression.type(), Arrays.asList(records));\n        ByteBufferOutputStream bufferStream = new ByteBufferOutputStream(sizeEstimate);\n        long logAppendTime = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            logAppendTime = System.currentTimeMillis();\n        try (final MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(bufferStream, magic, compression, timestampType,\n                initialOffset, logAppendTime, producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional, false,\n                partitionLeaderEpoch, sizeEstimate)) {\n            for (SimpleRecord record : records)\n                builder.append(record);\n            return builder.build();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create {@code MemoryRecords} with an end transaction marker.\n     *\n     * @param producerId The producer ID\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer epoch\n     * @param marker The end transaction marker\n     * @return {@code MemoryRecords} containing the marker\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withEndTransactionMarker(long producerId, short producerEpoch, EndTransactionMarker marker) {\n        return withEndTransactionMarker(0L, System.currentTimeMillis(), RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH,\n                producerId, producerEpoch, marker);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create {@code MemoryRecords} with end transaction marker and timestamp.\n     *\n     * @param timestamp The timestamp for the marker\n     * @param producerId The producer ID\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer epoch\n     * @param marker The end transaction marker\n     * @return {@code MemoryRecords} containing the marker\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withEndTransactionMarker(long timestamp, long producerId, short producerEpoch,\n                                                         EndTransactionMarker marker) {\n        return withEndTransactionMarker(0L, timestamp,  *\n     * @param initialOffset The base offset\n     * @param timestamp The timestamp for the marker\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param producerId The producer ID\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer epoch\n     * @param marker The end transaction marker\n     * @return {@code MemoryRecords} containing the marker\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withEndTransactionMarker(long initialOffset, long timestamp, int partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                                                         long producerId, short producerEpoch,\n                                                         EndTransactionMarker marker) {\n        int endTxnMarkerBatchSize = DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD + marker.endTxnMarkerValueSize();\n        ByteBuffer buffer = ByteBuffer.allocate(endTxnMarkerBatchSize);\n        writeEndTransactionalMarker(buffer, initialOffset, timestamp, partitionLeaderEpoch, producerId,\n                producerEpoch, marker);\n        buffer.flip();\n        return MemoryRecords.readableRecords(buffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write an end transaction marker to a buffer.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param initialOffset The base offset\n     * @param timestamp The timestamp for the marker\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param producerId The producer ID\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer epoch\n     * @param marker The end transaction marker\n     */\n    public static void writeEndTransactionalMarker(ByteBuffer buffer, long initialOffset, long timestamp,\n                                                   int partitionLeaderEpoch, long producerId, short producerEpoch,\n                                                   EndTransactionMarker marker) {\n        boolean isTransactional = true;\n        try (MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, Compression.NONE,\n                TimestampType.CREATE_TIME, initialOffset, timestamp, producerId, producerEpoch,\n                RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, isTransactional, true, partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                buffer.capacity())\n        ) {\n            builder.appendEndTxnMarker(timestamp, marker);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create {@code MemoryRecords} with a leader change message.\n     *\n     * @param initialOffset The base offset\n     * @param timestamp The timestamp for the message\n     * @param leaderEpoch The leader epoch\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param leaderChangeMessage The leader change message\n     * @return {@code MemoryRecords} containing the message\n     */\n    public static ) {\n        try (MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = createKraftControlRecordBuilder(\n                initialOffset,\n                timestamp,\n                leaderEpoch,\n                buffer\n The documentation covers the binary encoding and metadata handling for Kafka message batches, which are critical for protocol correctness and performance.\n\n## Documented Classes\n\n### 1. **RecordBatch.java** - Interface (Read-Only)\n\n**Purpose:** Defines the contract for accessing batch-level metadata and records in the Kafka protocol.\n\n**Key Documentation Additions:**\n\n- **Class-Level Javadoc:** Comprehensive explanation of batch containers across format versions (v0, v1, v2+), roles in the Kafka protocol, and usage patterns.\n\n- **Thread-Safety Statement:**\n  > \"Implementations of this interface are not thread-safe. Producer State Preservation\nExplanation of why offsets/sequences must be preserved during compaction:\n- Prevents OutOfOrderSequence errors\n- Maintains producer idempotence guarantees\n- Enables transaction recovery\n\n### 3. Timestamp Field Dual Purpose\n- **Normal case**: First and max timestamps of records\n- **Delete horizon case**: Time when tombstones should be removed\n\n### 4. Iterator Performance Tradeoff\n- `iterator()`: Decompresses full batch (higher memory)\n- `streamingIterator()`: Defers decompression (complex usage)\n\n### 5. Lazy Evaluation Pattern\nEmphasizes that batch parsing is deferred until:\n- `batchIterator()` called\n- `batches()` accessed\n- `filterTo()` invoked\n\n## Recommendations for Users\n\nBased on documentation added:\n\n1. **For Reading Batches**: Use `MemoryRecords.readableRecords()` and iterate via `batchIterator()`\n2. **For Writing Batches**: Use `MemoryRecords.builder()` factory methods\n3. **For Filtering**: Implement `RecordFilter` for custom retention policies\n4. **For Streaming**: Use `streamingIterator()` with `BufferSupplier.create()` for memory efficiency\n5. **For Compressed Data**: Be aware of decompression overhead - reuse buffers when possible\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThe Javadoc documentation comprehensively covers:\n- \u2705 Class purposes and roles in Kafka protocol\n- \u2705 Thread-safety guarantees for all classes\n- \u2705 Performance characteristics and tradeoffs\n- \u2705 Binary format specification and semantics\n- \u2705 All public methods with @param/@return/@throws\n- \u2705 Cross-references for navigation\n- \u2705 30+ factory method variants\n- \u2705 Compaction and state preservation semantics\n- \u2705 Iterator patterns and memory tradeoffs\n\nThe documentation enables developers to:\n- Understand Kafka's record batch protocol\n- Use the API efficiently and correctly\n- Avoid common concurrency and performance pitfalls\n- Implement custom filtering and transformation logic\n- Debug batch serialization issues\n",

/**
 * A record batch is a container for records in the Kafka protocol. It defines the binary encoding
 * and metadata for a group of messages sent as a unit.
 *
 * <p>In older versions of the record format (magic versions 0 and 1), a batch consisted of a single record
 * if no compression was enabled, but could contain many records when compression was used. Newer versions
 * (magic version 2 and above) generally contain many records regardless of compression.
 *
 * <p>This interface provides access to batch-level metadata such as:
 * <ul>
 *   <li>Offsets: base offset, last offset, and offset deltas for individual records</li>
 *   <li>Timestamps: base timestamp, 
... (truncated)

# Kafka Record Batch Serialization Javadoc Documentation

## Summary

This document describes the comprehensive Javadoc comments added to Kafka's record batch serialization classes in `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/record/internal/`. The documentation covers the binary encoding and metadata handling for Kafka message batches, which are critical for protocol correctness and performance.

## Documented Classes

### 1. **RecordBatch.java** - Interface (Read-Only)

**Purpose:** Defines the contract for accessing batch-level metadata and records in the Kafka protocol.

**Key Documentation Additions:**

- **Class-Level Javadoc:** Comprehensive explanation of batch containers across format versions (v0, v1, v2+), roles in the Kafka protocol, and usage patterns.

- **Thread-Safety Statement:**
  > "Implementations of this interface are not thread-safe. Callers must ensure that batches are not accessed concurrently from multiple threads."

- **Lazy Evaluation Warning:**
  > "Some operations, particularly `offsetOfMaxTimestamp()`, require full iteration over records and should be used with care in performance-critical code."

- **Method Documentation:** All 28 public methods documented with:
  - Purpose and behavior
  - `@return` tags describing return values and special cases (e.g., null for magic v0/v1)
  - `@throws` tags for exceptions
  - `{@link}` cross-references to related classes
  - Performance notes where relevant

**Notable Method Docs:**

- **`checksum()`**: Documents CRC-32C polynomial and coverage (attributes to batch end)
- **`baseOffset()`**: Explains deep iteration requirement for older magic versions with performance warning
- **`magic()`**: Documents all three magic versions (0, 1, 2) with their characteristics
- **`streamingIterator(BufferSuppl
... (truncated)
